    %busybox sed 's/%orig_var_name\([^_a-zA-Z0-9]\)/%new_var_name\1/g' | \
    
    %busybox tr '\f' '\n' > %temp_file Timeout (Seconds):0 Use Root:Off Store Output In: Store Errors In: Store Result In: Continue Task After Error:On ]

    - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br><br>
    Standard process limit (-1) could be 10, 15, 20, or whatever the Android manages in the background. In depends on your system.<br><br>
    Even 1, 2, 3 or 4 are the only available options to be chosen from settings (Developer Options), you can specify any other value higher than 4 if want too. (But, doing so will make the custom values not to be reflected on its settings, only visible by this task)>

Task:     ACCB - Setup (614)
    	<This is the task you have to configure to customize how the project works.>
    	A1: Anchor 
    	<<b>Cache Type:</b> The type of app's cache to act on. Config: 1 (user apps), 2 (system apps), 3 (all apps)<br><br>
    <b>Internal Storage</b> Whatever to act or not on the internal public storage. Config: auto (auto-path, clean cache), int_path (manual-path, clean cache).<br><br>
    <b>External Storage</b>: Whatever to act or not on the SDCard (external public storage), if any. Config: auto (auto-path, clean cache), sd_path (manual-path, clean cache), off (skip cache)<br><br>
    <b>Exclude Apps</b>: App(s) to be skipped from being cleaned. Config: app_pkg (skip app), off (full cleanup).<br><br>
    <b>Include Apps</b>: App(s) to be cleaned (the rest will be ignored). Config: app_pkg (clean app), off (full cleanup)<br><br>
    <b>Generate Log</b>: Generates a detailed log when the process finishes. Config: on (enable) , off (disable).<br><br>
    - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - -<br><br>
    <b>Cache Type</b>: The whole cleaning process will be fully dependent on this setting.<br><br>
    <b>Internal/External Storage</b>: If Tasker fails to get some of the paths automatically, set them here (absolute path).<br><br>
    <b>Exclude/Include Apps</b>: If any of the them is set (not <i>off</i>), the cleaning process will be based on how it was configured. Only one of them can be used at a time (or Exclude, or Include). Otherwise, if both are set (not <i>off</i>), 'Include Apps' will have preference. To add several packages separate each with '/' (pkg1/pkg2/...).<br><br>
    <b>Generate Log</b>: If enabled, all historical logs (+ current) will be saved and kept under <i>/... /Tasker/Resources/Apps Cache Cleaner/*</i> dir.<br><br>>
    	A2: Anchor 
    	<Cache Type>
    	A3: Variable Set [ Name:%var1 To:3 Recurse Variables:Off Do Maths:Off Append:Off Max Rounding Digits:3 ] 
    	<Internal Storage>
    	A4: Variable Set [ Name:%var2 To:auto Recurse Variables:Off Do Maths:Off Append:Off Max Rounding Digits:3 ] 
    	<External Storage>
    	A5: Variable Set [ Name:%var3 To:off Recurse Variables:Off Do Maths:Off Append:Off Max Rounding Digits:3 ] 
    	<Exclude Apps>
    	A6: Variable Set [ Name:%var4 To:net.dinglisch.android.taskerm/net.dinglisch.android.appfactory Recurse Variables:Off Do Maths:Off Append:Off Max Rounding Digits:3 ] 
    	<Include Apps>
    	A7: Variable Set [ Name:%var5 To:off Recurse Variables:Off Do Maths:Off Append:Off Max Rounding Digits:3 ]
